@@ -9,6 +9,65 @@ and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0
 
 ### Added
 
+- Makefile with development commands: `test`, `dev`, `deploy`, `schema`, and `help` targets
+- Hook script (`hooks/horizon-hook`) for Claude Code integration:
+  - Reads configuration from `~/.config/horizon/config.json`
+  - Extracts session_id from stdin JSON, generates if missing
+  - Determines project from git remote URL, fallback to directory basename
+  - Normalizes project name (lowercase, hyphens)
+  - Sends JSON payload to API with 5-second timeout
+  - Logs errors to `~/.config/horizon/error.log`
+  - Always exits 0 regardless of API failures
+- Hook configuration templates:
+  - `hooks/config.example.json` - placeholder config for API URL and key
+  - `hooks/settings.json.example` - Claude Code hook configuration for UserPromptSubmit, Stop, and SessionEnd events
+
+- Dashboard static site (`dashboard/`) with Ground Control theme:
+  - `index.html` - single-page app with header, stats cards, weekly activity, projects panel, session detail, and agents panels
+  - `styles.css` - dark theme (#0a0c10), amber accents (#e5a84b), IBM Plex Mono and Outfit fonts, responsive layout
+  - `config.js` - API_URL placeholder for deployment configuration
+  - `app.js` - state management, API key setup flow (localStorage), data fetching with caching, offline fallback, auto-refresh every 5 minutes, render functions for all panels, project selection with session loading, tooltips for weekly activity bars
+
+- API routes for interactions and statistics:
+  - `POST /api/interactions` - records interactions with validation for required fields, event_type, and ISO 8601 timestamp format; uses ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING for idempotency
+  - `GET /api/stats/weekly` - returns weekly statistics with optional `week_start` parameter
+  - `GET /api/stats/projects` - returns project statistics with optional `days` parameter (default 30)
+  - `GET /api/projects/:name/sessions` - returns sessions for a project with optional `days` parameter (default 7); returns 404 for non-existent projects
+- Main entry point (`src/index.ts`) wired with CORS middleware (configurable origin), API key authentication, route mounting, and global error handler that returns HTTP 500 with sanitized error messages while logging full context
+
+- Authentication middleware (`src/middleware/auth.ts`) that validates `x-api-key` header against environment secret, returning 401 for missing key and 403 for invalid key
+- Statistics service (`src/services/statistics.ts`) with:
+  - `calculateWeeklyStats` - aggregates interactions into weekly statistics
+  - `calculateDailyBreakdown` - generates 7-day breakdown with hours and session counts
+  - `calculateProjectBreakdown` - aggregates sessions by project, sorted by hours
+  - `calculateAgentBreakdown` - aggregates sessions by agent with percentages
+  - `calculateStreak` - counts consecutive days with coding activity
+- Unit tests for statistics calculation (`src/services/statistics.test.ts`) covering:
+  - Weekly totals calculation
+  - Daily breakdown generation for 7 days
+  - Project aggregation and sorting
+  - Agent aggregation with percentages
+  - Streak calculation with gap handling
+
+- Session derivation service (`src/services/sessions.ts`) with:
+  - `calculateSessions` - groups interactions by session_id and derives sessions
+  - `deriveSession` - calculates session properties from events
+  - `calculateActiveTime` - sums paired prompt-response durations with clock skew protection
+- Unit tests for session derivation (`src/services/sessions.test.ts`) covering:
+  - Normal prompt-response pairs
+  - 5-minute default for unpaired prompt-start
+  - Explicit session-end handling
+  - Out-of-order events processing
+  - Consecutive prompt-starts pairing
+  - Orphaned response-end events ignored
+  - Multiple sessions
+
+- TypeScript type definitions (`src/types.ts`) with EventType, Interaction, Session, WeeklyStats, DailyBreakdown, ProjectSummary, AgentSummary, and ProjectStats interfaces
+- Project setup with TypeScript, Hono, Wrangler, and Vitest
+- Database schema (`schema.sql`) with interactions table and indexes for idempotency
+- Vitest configuration for Cloudflare Workers pool
+- Minimal Hono entry point (`src/index.ts`)
+
 - Complete specification documents for Horizon v1:
   - Requirements document (`specs/horizon-v1/requirements.md`) with 19 user stories and 87 acceptance criteria in EARS format
   - Technical design document (`specs/horizon-v1/design.md`) covering architecture, components, data models, and testing strategy

+.PHONY: test dev deploy schema help
+
+help: ## Show this help
+	@grep -E '^[a-zA-Z_-]+:.*?## .*$$' $(MAKEFILE_LIST) | sort | awk 'BEGIN {FS = ":.*?## "}; {printf "\033[36m%-15s\033[0m %s\n", $$1, $$2}'
+
+test: ## Run all tests
+	npm test
+
+dev: ## Start development server
+	npm run dev
+
+deploy: ## Deploy to Cloudflare Workers
+	npm run deploy
+
+schema: ## Initialize D1 database schema
+	wrangler d1 execute horizon --file=schema.sql

@@ -0,0 +1,396 @@
+// Horizon Dashboard Application
+
+const CACHE_KEY = 'horizon_cache';
+const API_KEY_KEY = 'horizon_api_key';
+const REFRESH_INTERVAL = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5 minutes
+
+const PROJECT_COLORS = ['#e5a84b', '#4bc5e5', '#a84be5', '#4be5a8', '#e54b7c'];
+const AGENT_CONFIG = {
+  'claude-code': { name: 'Claude Code', class: 'claude', icon: 'C' },
+  'claude': { name: 'Claude', class: 'claude', icon: 'C' },
+  'cursor': { name: 'Cursor', class: 'cursor', icon: 'Cu' },
+  'copilot': { name: 'GitHub Copilot', class: 'copilot', icon: 'Co' },
+  'aider': { name: 'Aider', class: 'aider', icon: 'A' },
+};
+
+const state = {
+  weeklyStats: null,
+  selectedProject: null,
+  projectSessions: [],
+  lastSync: null,
+  isOffline: false,
+  apiKey: localStorage.getItem(API_KEY_KEY),
+};
+
+// Initialize
+document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
+
+async function init() {
+  if (!state.apiKey) {
+    showApiKeySetup();
+    return;
+  }
+  document.getElementById('api-key-modal').classList.add('hidden');
+  await loadWeeklyStats();
+  setInterval(loadWeeklyStats, REFRESH_INTERVAL);
+}
+
+function showApiKeySetup() {
+  const modal = document.getElementById('api-key-modal');
+  modal.classList.remove('hidden');
+
+  const input = document.getElementById('api-key-input');
+  const submit = document.getElementById('api-key-submit');
+
+  submit.addEventListener('click', () => {
+    const key = input.value.trim();
+    if (key) {
+      localStorage.setItem(API_KEY_KEY, key);
+      state.apiKey = key;
+      modal.classList.add('hidden');
+      loadWeeklyStats();
+    }
+  });
+
+  input.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
+    if (e.key === 'Enter') submit.click();
+  });
+}
+
+async function loadWeeklyStats() {
+  try {
+    const response = await fetch(`${CONFIG.API_URL}/api/stats/weekly`, {
+      headers: { 'x-api-key': state.apiKey },
+    });
+
+    if (!response.ok) throw new Error('API error');
+
+    state.weeklyStats = await response.json();
+    state.lastSync = new Date();
+    state.isOffline = false;
+
+    localStorage.setItem(CACHE_KEY, JSON.stringify({
+      weeklyStats: state.weeklyStats,
+      cachedAt: state.lastSync.toISOString(),
+    }));
+
+    render();
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Failed to load stats:', error);
+    loadFromCache();
+  }
+}
+
+function loadFromCache() {
+  const cached = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(CACHE_KEY) || '{}');
+  if (cached.weeklyStats) {
+    state.weeklyStats = cached.weeklyStats;
+    state.lastSync = new Date(cached.cachedAt);
+    state.isOffline = true;
+  }
+  render();
+}
+
+function render() {
+  renderSyncStatus();
+  renderStatsCards();
+  renderWeeklyActivity();
+  renderProjectsList();
+  renderAgentBreakdown();
+  renderAgentProjectList();
+}
+
+function renderSyncStatus() {
+  const dot = document.getElementById('sync-dot');
+  const text = document.getElementById('sync-text');
+
+  if (state.isOffline) {
+    dot.classList.add('offline');
+    text.textContent = 'offline';
+  } else if (state.lastSync) {
+    dot.classList.remove('offline');
+    const mins = Math.floor((Date.now() - state.lastSync.getTime()) / 60000);
+    text.textContent = mins < 1 ? 'synced just now' : `synced ${mins}m ago`;
+  }
+
+  // Set machine badge from first session if available
+  const machine = document.getElementById('machine-badge');
+  if (state.weeklyStats?.projects?.[0]) {
+    machine.textContent = 'dashboard';
+  }
+}
+
+function renderStatsCards() {
+  const stats = state.weeklyStats;
+  if (!stats) return;
+
+  document.getElementById('stat-week-hours').textContent = stats.total_hours?.toFixed(1) || '0';
+
+  const comparison = document.getElementById('stat-week-comparison');
+  const diff = stats.comparison?.vs_last_week || 0;
+  if (diff > 0) {
+    comparison.textContent = `↑ ${diff.toFixed(1)}hrs vs last week`;
+    comparison.className = 'stat-sub positive';
+  } else if (diff < 0) {
+    comparison.textContent = `↓ ${Math.abs(diff).toFixed(1)}hrs vs last week`;
+    comparison.className = 'stat-sub negative';
+  } else {
+    comparison.textContent = 'same as last week';
+    comparison.className = 'stat-sub';
+  }
+
+  // Today stats
+  const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
+  const todayData = stats.daily_breakdown?.find(d => d.date === today);
+  document.getElementById('stat-today-hours').textContent = todayData?.hours?.toFixed(1) || '0';
+  document.getElementById('stat-today-sessions').textContent =
+    `${todayData?.sessions || 0} session${todayData?.sessions !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
+
+  // Top agent
+  const topAgent = stats.agents?.[0];
+  if (topAgent) {
+    const agentInfo = AGENT_CONFIG[topAgent.name] || { name: topAgent.name };
+    document.getElementById('stat-top-agent').textContent = agentInfo.name;
+    document.getElementById('stat-top-agent-hours').textContent = `${topAgent.hours.toFixed(1)}hrs this week`;
+  }
+
+  // Streak
+  document.getElementById('stat-streak').textContent = stats.streak_days || 0;
+}
+
+function renderWeeklyActivity() {
+  const container = document.getElementById('weekly-timeline');
+  const stats = state.weeklyStats;
+  if (!stats?.daily_breakdown) {
+    container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No activity data</div>';
+    return;
+  }
+
+  const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
+  const maxHours = Math.max(...stats.daily_breakdown.map(d => d.hours), 1);
+
+  // Build project color map
+  const projectColors = {};
+  stats.projects?.forEach((p, i) => {
+    projectColors[p.name] = PROJECT_COLORS[i % PROJECT_COLORS.length];
+  });
+
+  container.innerHTML = stats.daily_breakdown.map(day => {
+    const date = new Date(day.date + 'T00:00:00Z');
+    const dayName = date.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'short', timeZone: 'UTC' });
+    const dayNum = date.getUTCDate();
+    const isToday = day.date === today;
+
+    // For segments, we need project breakdown per day
+    // Since API doesn't provide this, show single bar proportional to hours
+    const widthPercent = (day.hours / maxHours) * 100;
+    const color = PROJECT_COLORS[0];
+
+    return `
+      <div class="day-row">
+        <div class="day-label${isToday ? ' today' : ''}">${dayName} ${dayNum}</div>
+        <div class="day-bar-container">
+          <div class="day-segments">
+            ${day.hours > 0 ? `<div class="segment" style="width: ${widthPercent}%; background: ${color};" data-hours="${day.hours.toFixed(1)}"></div>` : ''}
+          </div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="day-hours">${day.hours.toFixed(1)}h</div>
+      </div>
+    `;
+  }).join('');
+
+  setupTooltips();
+}
+
+function renderProjectsList() {
+  const container = document.getElementById('project-list');
+  const stats = state.weeklyStats;
+  if (!stats?.projects?.length) {
+    container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No projects this week</div>';
+    return;
+  }
+
+  container.innerHTML = stats.projects.map((project, i) => {
+    const color = PROJECT_COLORS[i % PROJECT_COLORS.length];
+    const isActive = state.selectedProject === project.name;
+    return `
+      <div class="project-item${isActive ? ' active' : ''}" data-project="${project.name}">
+        <div class="project-color" style="background: ${color}"></div>
+        <div class="project-info">
+          <div class="project-name">${project.name}</div>
+          <div class="project-sessions">${project.sessions} session${project.sessions !== 1 ? 's' : ''}</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="project-hours">${project.hours.toFixed(1)}h</div>
+      </div>
+    `;
+  }).join('');
+
+  container.querySelectorAll('.project-item').forEach(item => {
+    item.addEventListener('click', () => selectProject(item.dataset.project));
+  });
+}
+
+async function selectProject(projectName) {
+  state.selectedProject = projectName;
+
+  // Update active state
+  document.querySelectorAll('.project-item').forEach(item => {
+    item.classList.toggle('active', item.dataset.project === projectName);
+  });
+
+  // Load sessions for this project
+  try {
+    const response = await fetch(`${CONFIG.API_URL}/api/projects/${encodeURIComponent(projectName)}/sessions?days=1`, {
+      headers: { 'x-api-key': state.apiKey },
+    });
+
+    if (response.ok) {
+      const data = await response.json();
+      state.projectSessions = data.sessions || [];
+      renderSessionDetail();
+    }
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Failed to load sessions:', error);
+  }
+}
+
+function renderSessionDetail() {
+  const container = document.getElementById('session-detail');
+  if (!state.selectedProject) {
+    container.classList.add('hidden');
+    return;
+  }
+
+  container.classList.remove('hidden');
+
+  const projectIndex = state.weeklyStats?.projects?.findIndex(p => p.name === state.selectedProject) || 0;
+  const color = PROJECT_COLORS[projectIndex % PROJECT_COLORS.length];
+
+  const sessionsHtml = state.projectSessions.length
+    ? state.projectSessions.map(session => {
+        const start = new Date(session.start);
+        const startTime = start.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', hour12: false });
+        const endTime = session.end
+          ? new Date(session.end).toLocaleTimeString('en-US', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', hour12: false })
+          : 'now';
+        const duration = session.end
+          ? formatDuration(session.active_minutes)
+          : 'active';
+        const agentInfo = AGENT_CONFIG[session.agent] || { class: 'claude', name: session.agent };
+
+        return `
+          <div class="session-entry">
+            <span class="session-time">${startTime} — ${endTime}</span>
+            <span class="session-agent ${agentInfo.class}">
+              <span class="session-agent-dot"></span>
+              ${agentInfo.name.toLowerCase().split(' ')[0]}
+            </span>
+            <span class="session-duration">${duration}</span>
+            <span class="session-machine">${session.machine}</span>
+          </div>
+        `;
+      }).join('')
+    : '<div class="empty-state">No sessions today</div>';
+
+  container.innerHTML = `
+    <div class="session-detail-header">
+      <div class="project-color" style="background: ${color}"></div>
+      <div class="session-detail-title">${state.selectedProject} sessions today</div>
+    </div>
+    <div class="session-list">${sessionsHtml}</div>
+  `;
+}
+
+function renderAgentBreakdown() {
+  const container = document.getElementById('agent-breakdown');
+  const stats = state.weeklyStats;
+  if (!stats?.agents?.length) {
+    container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No agent data</div>';
+    return;
+  }
+
+  container.innerHTML = stats.agents.map(agent => {
+    const agentInfo = AGENT_CONFIG[agent.name] || { class: 'claude', name: agent.name };
+    const showHours = agent.percentage >= 15;
+    return `
+      <div class="agent-breakdown-row">
+        <div class="agent-breakdown-label">
+          <span class="agent-breakdown-dot ${agentInfo.class}"></span>
+          ${agentInfo.name.split(' ')[0]}
+        </div>
+        <div class="agent-breakdown-bar">
+          <div class="agent-breakdown-fill ${agentInfo.class}" style="width: ${agent.percentage}%;">
+            ${showHours ? agent.hours.toFixed(1) + 'h' : ''}
+          </div>
+        </div>
+        <span class="agent-breakdown-value">${agent.percentage}%</span>
+      </div>
+    `;
+  }).join('');
+}
+
+function renderAgentProjectList() {
+  const container = document.getElementById('agent-project-list');
+  const stats = state.weeklyStats;
+  if (!stats?.agents?.length) {
+    container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No agent data</div>';
+    return;
+  }
+
+  // Build agent-to-projects mapping from projects data
+  const agentProjects = {};
+  stats.agents.forEach(a => { agentProjects[a.name] = []; });
+
+  // Since we don't have per-project agent breakdown, show all projects for each agent
+  const projectNames = stats.projects?.map(p => p.name).slice(0, 3).join(', ') || '—';
+
+  container.innerHTML = stats.agents.map(agent => {
+    const agentInfo = AGENT_CONFIG[agent.name] || { class: 'claude', name: agent.name, icon: agent.name[0].toUpperCase() };
+    return `
+      <div class="agent-item">
+        <div class="agent-icon ${agentInfo.class}">${agentInfo.icon}</div>
+        <div class="agent-info">
+          <div class="agent-name">${agentInfo.name}</div>
+          <div class="agent-sessions">${projectNames}</div>
+        </div>
+        <div class="agent-hours">${agent.hours.toFixed(1)}h</div>
+      </div>
+    `;
+  }).join('');
+}
+
+function setupTooltips() {
+  const tooltip = document.getElementById('tooltip');
+  const segments = document.querySelectorAll('.segment');
+
+  segments.forEach(seg => {
+    seg.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
+      const hours = seg.dataset.hours;
+      if (hours) {
+        tooltip.innerHTML = `
+          <div class="tooltip-row">
+            <span class="tooltip-label">Hours</span>
+            <span>${hours}h</span>
+          </div>
+        `;
+        tooltip.classList.add('visible');
+      }
+    });
+
+    seg.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
+      tooltip.style.left = e.pageX + 10 + 'px';
+      tooltip.style.top = e.pageY - 30 + 'px';
+    });
+
+    seg.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
+      tooltip.classList.remove('visible');
+    });
+  });
+}
+
+function formatDuration(minutes) {
+  if (minutes < 60) return `${Math.round(minutes)}m`;
+  const h = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
+  const m = Math.round(minutes % 60);
+  return m > 0 ? `${h}h ${m}m` : `${h}h`;
+}

+};

+</head>
+<body>

+
+    <header>

+          </svg>
+        </div>

+      </div>
+      <div class="header-meta">
+        <div class="sync-status">
+          <span id="sync-dot" class="sync-dot"></span>
+          <span id="sync-text">syncing...</span>
+        </div>

+

+      </div>

+      </div>

+      </div>
+      <div class="stat-card">
+        <div class="stat-label">Streak</div>
+        <div class="stat-value"><span id="stat-streak">—</span><span class="unit">days</span></div>
+        <div class="stat-sub">consecutive days</div>
+      </div>

+
+    <div class="main-grid">
+      <div class="panel">

diff --git a/hooks/horizon-hook b/hooks/horizon-hook
new file mode 100755
index 0000000..a30e095
--- /dev/null
+++ b/hooks/horizon-hook
@@ -0,0 +1,81 @@
+#!/bin/bash
+# Horizon hook script for Claude Code integration
+# Install to: ~/.local/bin/horizon-hook
+
+CONFIG_FILE="$HOME/.config/horizon/config.json"
+LOG_FILE="$HOME/.config/horizon/error.log"
+EVENT_TYPE="${1:-prompt-start}"
+
+mkdir -p "$(dirname "$LOG_FILE")"
+
+log_error() {
+    echo "$(date -u +%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ) - $1" >> "$LOG_FILE"
+}
+
+# Read hook input from stdin
+HOOK_INPUT=$(cat)
+
+# Extract session_id from hook input, generate if missing
+SESSION_ID=$(echo "$HOOK_INPUT" | jq -r '.session_id // empty' 2>/dev/null)
+if [[ -z "$SESSION_ID" ]]; then
+    SESSION_ID="generated-$(date +%s)-$$"
+fi
+
+# Read config
+if [[ ! -f "$CONFIG_FILE" ]]; then
+    log_error "Config file not found: $CONFIG_FILE"
+    exit 0
+fi
+
+API_URL=$(jq -r '.api_url // empty' "$CONFIG_FILE")
+API_KEY=$(jq -r '.api_key // empty' "$CONFIG_FILE")
+
+if [[ -z "$API_URL" || -z "$API_KEY" ]]; then
+    log_error "Missing api_url or api_key in config"
+    exit 0
+fi
+
+# Determine project name from git remote, fallback to directory name
+PROJECT=""
+if git rev-parse --git-dir > /dev/null 2>&1; then
+    REMOTE_URL=$(git remote get-url origin 2>/dev/null || true)
+    if [[ -n "$REMOTE_URL" ]]; then
+        PROJECT=$(echo "$REMOTE_URL" | sed -E 's/.*[\/:]([^\/]+)(\.git)?$/\1/' | sed 's/\.git$//')
+    fi
+fi
+
+if [[ -z "$PROJECT" ]]; then
+    PROJECT=$(basename "$(pwd)")
+fi
+
+# Normalize project name: lowercase, hyphens for special chars
+PROJECT=$(echo "$PROJECT" | tr '[:upper:]' '[:lower:]' | sed 's/[^a-z0-9-]/-/g' | sed 's/--*/-/g')
+
+# Build payload
+TIMESTAMP=$(date -u +%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ)
+MACHINE=$(hostname -s)
+AGENT="claude-code"
+
+PAYLOAD=$(jq -n \
+    --arg project "$PROJECT" \
+    --arg timestamp "$TIMESTAMP" \
+    --arg machine "$MACHINE" \
+    --arg agent "$AGENT" \
+    --arg session_id "$SESSION_ID" \
+    --arg event_type "$EVENT_TYPE" \
+    '{project: $project, timestamp: $timestamp, machine: $machine, agent: $agent, session_id: $session_id, event_type: $event_type}')
+
+# Send to API (5-second timeout, silent failure)
+HTTP_CODE=$(curl -s -o /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" \
+    -X POST "$API_URL/api/interactions" \
+    -H "x-api-key: $API_KEY" \
+    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
+    -d "$PAYLOAD" \
+    --max-time 5 \
+    2>/dev/null) || HTTP_CODE="000"
+
+if [[ "$HTTP_CODE" != "201" && "$HTTP_CODE" != "200" ]]; then
+    log_error "API request failed with HTTP $HTTP_CODE for project=$PROJECT session=$SESSION_ID event=$EVENT_TYPE"
+fi
+
+exit 0

+        "timeout": 5000
+      }

diff --git a/schema.sql b/schema.sql
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..452b547
--- /dev/null
+++ b/schema.sql
@@ -0,0 +1,31 @@
+-- Interactions table
+CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS interactions (
+    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
+    project TEXT NOT NULL,
+    timestamp TEXT NOT NULL,
+    machine TEXT NOT NULL,
+    agent TEXT NOT NULL,
+    session_id TEXT NOT NULL,
+    event_type TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (event_type IN ('prompt-start', 'response-end', 'session-end')),
+    created_at TEXT DEFAULT (datetime('now'))
+);
+
+-- Unique constraint for idempotency
+CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_interactions_unique
+ON interactions(session_id, timestamp, event_type);
+
+-- Index for project + time range queries
+CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_interactions_project_timestamp
+ON interactions(project, timestamp DESC);
+
+-- Index for date-based queries
+CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_interactions_date
+ON interactions(date(timestamp), timestamp DESC);
+
+-- Index for session grouping
+CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_interactions_session
+ON interactions(session_id, timestamp ASC);
+
+-- Index for agent statistics
+CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_interactions_agent
+ON interactions(agent, timestamp DESC);

diff --git a/src/index.ts b/src/index.ts
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..b6680a6
--- /dev/null
+++ b/src/index.ts
@@ -0,0 +1,42 @@
+import { Hono } from 'hono';
+import { cors } from 'hono/cors';
+import { apiKeyAuth } from './middleware/auth';
+import interactionsRoutes from './routes/interactions';
+import statsRoutes from './routes/stats';
+
+export type Bindings = {
+  DB: D1Database;
+  API_KEY: string;
+  CORS_ORIGIN: string;
+};
+
+const app = new Hono<{ Bindings: Bindings }>();
+
+app.onError((err, c) => {
+  console.error(JSON.stringify({
+    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
+    endpoint: c.req.path,
+    method: c.req.method,
+    error_type: err.name,
+    message: err.message,
+  }));
+  return c.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, 500);
+});
+
+app.use('/api/*', async (c, next) => {
+  const corsMiddleware = cors({
+    origin: c.env.CORS_ORIGIN || '*',
+    allowHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'x-api-key'],
+    allowMethods: ['GET', 'POST', 'OPTIONS'],
+  });
+  return corsMiddleware(c, next);
+});
+
+app.use('/api/*', apiKeyAuth());
+
+app.route('/api', interactionsRoutes);
+app.route('/api', statsRoutes);
+
+app.get('/', (c) => c.text('Horizon API'));
+
+export default app;
diff --git a/src/middleware/auth.ts b/src/middleware/auth.ts
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..9cf91b1
--- /dev/null
+++ b/src/middleware/auth.ts
@@ -0,0 +1,18 @@
+import type { Context, Next } from 'hono';
+import type { Bindings } from '../index';
+
+export function apiKeyAuth() {
+  return async (c: Context<{ Bindings: Bindings }>, next: Next) => {
+    const apiKey = c.req.header('x-api-key');
+
+    if (!apiKey) {
+      return c.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, 401);
+    }
+
+    if (apiKey !== c.env.API_KEY) {
+      return c.json({ error: 'Forbidden' }, 403);
+    }
+
+    await next();
+  };
+}
diff --git a/src/routes/interactions.ts b/src/routes/interactions.ts
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..999ed75
--- /dev/null
+++ b/src/routes/interactions.ts
@@ -0,0 +1,48 @@
+import { Hono } from 'hono';
+import type { Bindings } from '../index';
+import type { EventType } from '../types';
+
+const VALID_EVENT_TYPES: EventType[] = ['prompt-start', 'response-end', 'session-end'];
+
+const app = new Hono<{ Bindings: Bindings }>();
+
+app.post('/interactions', async (c) => {
+  const body = await c.req.json();
+
+  const required = ['project', 'timestamp', 'machine', 'agent', 'session_id', 'event_type'] as const;
+  for (const field of required) {
+    if (!body[field]) {
+      return c.json({ error: `Missing required field: ${field}` }, 400);
+    }
+  }
+
+  if (!VALID_EVENT_TYPES.includes(body.event_type)) {
+    return c.json({ error: `Invalid event_type. Must be one of: ${VALID_EVENT_TYPES.join(', ')}` }, 400);
+  }
+
+  if (isNaN(Date.parse(body.timestamp))) {
+    return c.json({ error: 'Invalid timestamp format. Use ISO 8601.' }, 400);
+  }
+
+  try {
+    await c.env.DB.prepare(`
+      INSERT INTO interactions (project, timestamp, machine, agent, session_id, event_type)
+      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
+      ON CONFLICT (session_id, timestamp, event_type) DO NOTHING
+    `).bind(
+      body.project,
+      body.timestamp,
+      body.machine,
+      body.agent,
+      body.session_id,
+      body.event_type
+    ).run();
+
+    return c.json({ status: 'recorded' }, 201);
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Failed to record interaction:', error);
+    return c.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, 500);
+  }
+});
+
+export default app;
diff --git a/src/routes/stats.ts b/src/routes/stats.ts
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..96fa5ca
--- /dev/null
+++ b/src/routes/stats.ts
@@ -0,0 +1,105 @@
+import { Hono } from 'hono';
+import type { Bindings } from '../index';
+import type { Interaction, ProjectStats } from '../types';
+import { calculateSessions } from '../services/sessions';
+import { calculateWeeklyStats } from '../services/statistics';
+
+const app = new Hono<{ Bindings: Bindings }>();
+
+function getMonday(date: Date): Date {
+  const d = new Date(date);
+  const day = d.getUTCDay();
+  const diff = d.getUTCDate() - day + (day === 0 ? -6 : 1);
+  d.setUTCDate(diff);
+  d.setUTCHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
+  return d;
+}
+
+app.get('/stats/weekly', async (c) => {
+  const weekStartParam = c.req.query('week_start');
+  const weekStart = weekStartParam
+    ? new Date(weekStartParam + 'T00:00:00Z')
+    : getMonday(new Date());
+
+  const weekEnd = new Date(weekStart);
+  weekEnd.setUTCDate(weekEnd.getUTCDate() + 7);
+
+  const { results } = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
+    SELECT * FROM interactions
+    WHERE timestamp >= ? AND timestamp < ?
+    ORDER BY timestamp ASC
+  `).bind(weekStart.toISOString(), weekEnd.toISOString()).all();
+
+  const stats = calculateWeeklyStats(results as unknown as Interaction[], weekStart);
+  return c.json(stats);
+});
+
+app.get('/stats/projects', async (c) => {
+  const days = parseInt(c.req.query('days') || '30');
+  const startDate = new Date();
+  startDate.setUTCDate(startDate.getUTCDate() - days);
+  startDate.setUTCHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
+
+  const { results } = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
+    SELECT * FROM interactions
+    WHERE timestamp >= ?
+    ORDER BY timestamp ASC
+  `).bind(startDate.toISOString()).all();
+
+  const sessions = calculateSessions(results as unknown as Interaction[]);
+
+  const projectMap = new Map<string, ProjectStats>();
+  for (const session of sessions) {
+    const existing = projectMap.get(session.project) || {
+      name: session.project,
+      total_hours: 0,
+      total_sessions: 0,
+      agents: {},
+    };
+    existing.total_hours += session.active_minutes / 60;
+    existing.total_sessions += 1;
+    existing.agents[session.agent] = (existing.agents[session.agent] || 0) + session.active_minutes / 60;
+    projectMap.set(session.project, existing);
+  }
+
+  const projects = Array.from(projectMap.values())
+    .map(p => ({
+      ...p,
+      total_hours: Math.round(p.total_hours * 10) / 10,
+      agents: Object.fromEntries(
+        Object.entries(p.agents).map(([k, v]) => [k, Math.round(v * 10) / 10])
+      ),
+    }))
+    .sort((a, b) => b.total_hours - a.total_hours);
+
+  return c.json({ projects });
+});
+
+app.get('/projects/:name/sessions', async (c) => {
+  const projectName = c.req.param('name');
+  const days = parseInt(c.req.query('days') || '7');
+  const startDate = new Date();
+  startDate.setUTCDate(startDate.getUTCDate() - days);
+  startDate.setUTCHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
+
+  const { results } = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
+    SELECT * FROM interactions
+    WHERE project = ? AND timestamp >= ?
+    ORDER BY timestamp ASC
+  `).bind(projectName, startDate.toISOString()).all();
+
+  if (results.length === 0) {
+    const { results: exists } = await c.env.DB.prepare(`
+      SELECT 1 FROM interactions WHERE project = ? LIMIT 1
+    `).bind(projectName).all();
+
+    if (exists.length === 0) {
+      return c.json({ error: 'Project not found' }, 404);
+    }
+  }
+
+  const sessions = calculateSessions(results as unknown as Interaction[]);
+  return c.json({ project: projectName, sessions });
+});
+
+export default app;
diff --git a/src/services/sessions.test.ts b/src/services/sessions.test.ts
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..b221e66

+++ b/src/services/sessions.test.ts
@@ -0,0 +1,170 @@
+import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest';
+import { calculateSessions, deriveSession, calculateActiveTime } from './sessions';
+import { Interaction, EventType } from '../types';
+
+function makeInteraction(
+  overrides: Partial<Interaction> & { timestamp: string; event_type: EventType }
+): Interaction {
+  return {
+    project: 'test-project',
+    machine: 'test-machine',
+    agent: 'claude-code',
+    session_id: 's1',
+    ...overrides,
+  };
+}
+
+describe('calculateSessions', () => {
+  it('calculates active time from paired prompt-response events', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:20:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+    ];
+    const sessions = calculateSessions(interactions);
+    expect(sessions).toHaveLength(1);
+    expect(sessions[0].active_minutes).toBe(20);
+  });
+
+  it('uses 5-minute default for unpaired prompt-start', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+    ];
+    const sessions = calculateSessions(interactions);
+    expect(sessions[0].active_minutes).toBe(5);
+  });
+
+  it('handles explicit session-end', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:20:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:30:00Z', event_type: 'session-end' }),
+    ];
+    const sessions = calculateSessions(interactions);
+    expect(sessions[0].explicit_end).toBe(true);
+    expect(sessions[0].end).toBe('2026-01-19T10:30:00.000Z');
+  });
+
+  it('processes events in timestamp order regardless of arrival order', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:20:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+    ];
+    const sessions = calculateSessions(interactions);
+    expect(sessions[0].active_minutes).toBe(20);
+    expect(sessions[0].start).toBe('2026-01-19T10:00:00Z');
+  });
+
+  it('pairs consecutive prompt-starts with next available response-ends', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:05:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:10:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:20:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+    ];
+    const sessions = calculateSessions(interactions);
+    // First prompt (10:00) pairs with first response (10:10) = 10 min
+    // Second prompt (10:05) pairs with second response (10:20) = 15 min
+    expect(sessions[0].active_minutes).toBe(25);
+  });
+
+  it('ignores orphaned response-end events', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:05:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:15:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+    ];
+    const sessions = calculateSessions(interactions);
+    // Only 10:05-10:15 pair counts
+    expect(sessions[0].active_minutes).toBe(10);
+  });
+
+  it('handles multiple sessions correctly', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ session_id: 's1', timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ session_id: 's2', timestamp: '2026-01-19T11:00:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ session_id: 's1', timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:30:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+      makeInteraction({ session_id: 's2', timestamp: '2026-01-19T11:10:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+    ];
+    const sessions = calculateSessions(interactions);
+    expect(sessions).toHaveLength(2);
+    // Sessions sorted by start descending
+    expect(sessions[0].session_id).toBe('s2');
+    expect(sessions[0].active_minutes).toBe(10);
+    expect(sessions[1].session_id).toBe('s1');
+    expect(sessions[1].active_minutes).toBe(30);
+  });
+
+  it('returns empty array for empty input', () => {
+    const sessions = calculateSessions([]);
+    expect(sessions).toHaveLength(0);
+  });
+
+  it('marks session as active when last prompt-start has no response-end', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:20:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:30:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+    ];
+    const sessions = calculateSessions(interactions);
+    expect(sessions[0].end).toBeNull();
+    // 20 min from first pair + 5 min default for unpaired
+    expect(sessions[0].active_minutes).toBe(25);
+  });
+
+  it('counts interaction_count as number of prompt-start events', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:10:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:15:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:25:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+    ];
+    const sessions = calculateSessions(interactions);
+    expect(sessions[0].interaction_count).toBe(2);
+  });
+});
+
+describe('calculateActiveTime', () => {
+  it('handles clock skew by clamping negative durations to zero', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:10:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:05:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+    ];
+    // response-end before prompt-start due to clock skew
+    const activeTime = calculateActiveTime(interactions);
+    expect(activeTime).toBe(0);
+  });
+});
+
+describe('deriveSession', () => {
+  it('calculates span_minutes from first to last event', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z', event_type: 'prompt-start' }),
+      makeInteraction({ timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:30:00Z', event_type: 'response-end' }),
+    ];
+    const session = deriveSession('s1', interactions);
+    expect(session.span_minutes).toBe(30);
+  });
+
+  it('uses first event metadata for session properties', () => {
+    const interactions = [
+      makeInteraction({
+        timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:00:00Z',
+        event_type: 'prompt-start',
+        project: 'my-project',
+        machine: 'laptop',
+        agent: 'claude-code',
+      }),
+      makeInteraction({
+        timestamp: '2026-01-19T10:30:00Z',
+        event_type: 'response-end',
+        project: 'my-project',
+        machine: 'laptop',
+        agent: 'claude-code',
+      }),
+    ];
+    const session = deriveSession('s1', interactions);
+    expect(session.project).toBe('my-project');
+    expect(session.machine).toBe('laptop');
+    expect(session.agent).toBe('claude-code');
+  });
+});
diff --git a/src/services/sessions.ts b/src/services/sessions.ts
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..c46cd12
--- /dev/null
+++ b/src/services/sessions.ts
@@ -0,0 +1,87 @@
+import { Interaction, Session } from '../types';
+
+const DEFAULT_DURATION_MINUTES = 5;
+
+export function calculateSessions(interactions: Interaction[]): Session[] {
+  if (interactions.length === 0) return [];
+
+  const grouped = new Map<string, Interaction[]>();
+  for (const interaction of interactions) {
+    const existing = grouped.get(interaction.session_id) || [];
+    existing.push(interaction);
+    grouped.set(interaction.session_id, existing);
+  }
+
+  const sessions: Session[] = [];
+  for (const [sessionId, events] of grouped) {
+    events.sort((a, b) =>
+      new Date(a.timestamp).getTime() - new Date(b.timestamp).getTime()
+    );
+    sessions.push(deriveSession(sessionId, events));
+  }
+
+  sessions.sort((a, b) =>
+    new Date(b.start).getTime() - new Date(a.start).getTime()
+  );
+
+  return sessions;
+}
+
+export function deriveSession(sessionId: string, events: Interaction[]): Session {
+  const firstEvent = events[0];
+  const lastEvent = events[events.length - 1];
+
+  const hasSessionEnd = events.some(e => e.event_type === 'session-end');
+  const lastPromptStart = [...events].reverse().find(e => e.event_type === 'prompt-start');
+  const hasMatchingResponseEnd = lastPromptStart
+    ? events.some(e =>
+        e.event_type === 'response-end' &&
+        new Date(e.timestamp) > new Date(lastPromptStart.timestamp)
+      )
+    : true;
+
+  const isActive = !hasSessionEnd && !hasMatchingResponseEnd;
+  const activeMinutes = calculateActiveTime(events);
+
+  const startTime = new Date(firstEvent.timestamp);
+  const endTime = isActive ? null : new Date(lastEvent.timestamp);
+  const spanMinutes = endTime
+    ? Math.round((endTime.getTime() - startTime.getTime()) / 60000)
+    : Math.round((Date.now() - startTime.getTime()) / 60000);
+
+  const interactionCount = events.filter(e => e.event_type === 'prompt-start').length;
+
+  return {
+    session_id: sessionId,
+    project: firstEvent.project,
+    start: firstEvent.timestamp,
+    end: endTime?.toISOString() ?? null,
+    span_minutes: spanMinutes,
+    active_minutes: activeMinutes,
+    machine: firstEvent.machine,
+    agent: firstEvent.agent,
+    interaction_count: interactionCount,
+    explicit_end: hasSessionEnd,
+  };
+}
+
+export function calculateActiveTime(events: Interaction[]): number {
+  let totalMinutes = 0;
+  const promptStarts: Interaction[] = [];
+
+  for (const event of events) {
+    if (event.event_type === 'prompt-start') {
+      promptStarts.push(event);
+    } else if (event.event_type === 'response-end') {
+      const promptStart = promptStarts.shift();
+      if (promptStart) {
+        const start = new Date(promptStart.timestamp).getTime();
+        const end = new Date(event.timestamp).getTime();
+        totalMinutes += Math.max(0, (end - start) / 60000);
+      }
+    }
+  }
+
+  totalMinutes += promptStarts.length * DEFAULT_DURATION_MINUTES;
+  return Math.round(totalMinutes * 10) / 10;
+}

+import { Interaction, Session, WeeklyStats, DailyBreakdown, ProjectSummary, AgentSummary } from '../types';
+import { calculateSessions } from './sessions';
+
+export function calculateWeeklyStats(interactions: Interaction[], weekStart: Date): WeeklyStats {
+  const sessions = calculateSessions(interactions);
+  const totalHours = sessions.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.active_minutes, 0) / 60;
+
+  return {
+    total_hours: Math.round(totalHours * 10) / 10,
+    total_sessions: sessions.length,
+    streak_days: calculateStreak(interactions),
+    daily_breakdown: calculateDailyBreakdown(sessions, weekStart),
+    projects: calculateProjectBreakdown(sessions),
+    agents: calculateAgentBreakdown(sessions, totalHours),
+    comparison: { vs_last_week: 0 },
+  };
+}
+
+export function calculateDailyBreakdown(sessions: Session[], weekStart: Date): DailyBreakdown[] {
+  const days: DailyBreakdown[] = [];
+
+  for (let i = 0; i < 7; i++) {
+    const date = new Date(weekStart);
+    date.setUTCDate(date.getUTCDate() + i);
+    const dateStr = date.toISOString().split('T')[0];
+
+    const daySessions = sessions.filter(s => s.start.startsWith(dateStr));
+    const hours = daySessions.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.active_minutes, 0) / 60;
+
+    days.push({
+      date: dateStr,
+      hours: Math.round(hours * 10) / 10,
+      sessions: daySessions.length,
+    });
+  }
+
+  return days;
+}
+
+export function calculateProjectBreakdown(sessions: Session[]): ProjectSummary[] {
+  const projectMap = new Map<string, { hours: number; sessions: number }>();
+
+  for (const session of sessions) {
+    const existing = projectMap.get(session.project) || { hours: 0, sessions: 0 };
+    existing.hours += session.active_minutes / 60;
+    existing.sessions += 1;
+    projectMap.set(session.project, existing);
+  }
+
+  return Array.from(projectMap.entries())
+    .map(([name, data]) => ({
+      name,
+      hours: Math.round(data.hours * 10) / 10,
+      sessions: data.sessions,
+    }))
+    .sort((a, b) => b.hours - a.hours);
+}
+
+export function calculateAgentBreakdown(sessions: Session[], totalHours: number): AgentSummary[] {
+  const agentMap = new Map<string, number>();
+
+  for (const session of sessions) {
+    const existing = agentMap.get(session.agent) || 0;
+    agentMap.set(session.agent, existing + session.active_minutes / 60);
+  }
+
+  return Array.from(agentMap.entries())
+    .map(([name, hours]) => ({
+      name,
+      hours: Math.round(hours * 10) / 10,
+      percentage: totalHours > 0 ? Math.round((hours / totalHours) * 100) : 0,
+    }))
+    .sort((a, b) => b.hours - a.hours);
+}
+
+export function calculateStreak(interactions: Interaction[], today: Date = new Date()): number {
+  if (interactions.length === 0) return 0;
+
+  const datesWithSessions = new Set<string>();
+  for (const interaction of interactions) {
+    datesWithSessions.add(interaction.timestamp.split('T')[0]);
+  }
+
+  let streak = 0;
+  const checkDate = new Date(today);
+  checkDate.setUTCHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
+
+  for (let i = 0; i < 365; i++) {
+    const dateStr = checkDate.toISOString().split('T')[0];
+
+    if (datesWithSessions.has(dateStr)) {
+      streak++;
+    } else if (i > 0) {
+      break;
+    }
+
+    checkDate.setUTCDate(checkDate.getUTCDate() - 1);
+  }
+
+  return streak;
+}

+export type EventType = 'prompt-start' | 'response-end' | 'session-end';
+
+export interface Interaction {
+  id?: number;
+  project: string;
+  timestamp: string;
+  machine: string;
+  agent: string;

+  created_at?: string;

+  active_minutes: number;
+  machine: string;

+}
